3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (19 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="searchinput" name="find" placeholder="Klikk her for å søke." type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<input data-index="0" data-level="1" id="hc-nav-1-1-0" type="checkbox" value="8ukvk3b9h6j-6im4c88wgut"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id
